# health_resources_va.csv

**Description:** Health Resources and Services Administration (HRSA) Area Health Resources Files (AHRF). This county-level dataset features longitudinal indicators tracking healthcare worker distribution, clinical facility assets, utilization trends, and regional economic characteristics across Virginia.

- **Source Organization:** Health Resources and Services Administration (HRSA)
- **Geographic Coverage:** County
- **Temporal Coverage:** 2024-2025
- **URL Source:** [Link]()
- **Spatial Alignment:** FIPS Column: `secndry_entity_file`, Locality Column: `cnty_name`

### Column Schema

* **`fips_st_cnty`** (**): [Category: GEO] Header - FIPS State & Cty Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`entity_file`** (**): [Category: GEO] Entity of File (Details: Equals 'AHRF ') *(Keywords: None)*
* **`secndry_entity_file`** (**): [Category: GEO] Secondary Entity Of File (Details: Mod FIPS State & Cty Code) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`date_file`** (**): [Category: GEO] Date of File (Details: Equals '2025') *(Keywords: None)*
* **`date_cretn`** (**): [Category: GEO] Date of Creation (Details: Equals '25725') *(Keywords: None)*
* **`file_length`** (**): [Category: GEO] File Length (Details: Equals '26288') *(Keywords: None)*
* **`st_name`** (**): [Category: GEO] State Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`st_name_abbrev`** (**): [Category: GEO] State Name Abbreviation *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cnty_name`** (**): [Category: GEO] County Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cnty_name_st_abbrev`** (**): [Category: GEO] County Name w/State Abbrev *(Keywords: None)*
* **`fips_st`** (**): [Category: GEO] FIPS State Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`fips_cnty`** (**): [Category: GEO] FIPS County Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cens_regn`** (**): [Category: GEO] Census Region Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cens_regn_name`** (**): [Category: GEO] Census Region Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cens_divsn`** (**): [Category: GEO] Census Division Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cens_divsn_name`** (**): [Category: GEO] Census Division Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`fed_regn`** (**): [Category: GEO] Federal Region Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`ssa_benfcry`** (**): [Category: GEO] SSA Beneficiary Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cbsa_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Core Based Stat Area Code(CBSA) (Details: Metropolitan/Micropolitan) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cbsa_name_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Core Based Stat Area Name(CBSA) (Details: Metropolitan/Micropolitan) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cbsa_ind_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] CBSA Indicator Code (Details: 0 = Not, 1 = Metro, 2 = Micro) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`cbsa_cnty_stats_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] CBSA County Status (Details: Central or Outlying) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`metro_divsn_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Metropolitan Division Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`metro_divsn_name_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Metropolitan Division Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`combnd_stat_area_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Combined Statistical Area Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`combnd_stat_area_name_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Combined Statistical Area Name *(Keywords: None)*
* **`rural_urban_contnm_23`** (**): [Category: GEO] Rural-Urban Continuum Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`urban_influnc_13`** (**): [Category: GEO] Urban Influence Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`econ_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Economic-Dependent Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`farmng_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Farming-Dependent Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`minng_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Mining-Dependent Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`mfg_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Manufacturing-Dependent Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`fed_st_govt_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Fed/State Govt-Dependent Typology Code (Details: Federal/State Government) *(Keywords: None)*
* **`recrtn_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Recreation Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`nonspclzd_depndnt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Nonspecialized-Dep Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`lo_eductn_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Low Education Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`lo_emplymt_typolgy_15`** (**): [Category: GEO] Low Employment Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`hi_povty_typolgy_14`** (**): [Category: GEO] High Poverty Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
* **`prstnt_povty_typolgy_14`** (**): [Category: GEO] Persistent Poverty Typology Code *(Keywords: None)*
